Z-Image Ideogram 4 Krea
Most Wanted: The Reckoning Round
Weird West x Reality Competition

In the cursed boomtown of Gallows Gulch, the law has been replaced by a hit reality show, and grizzled bounty hunter Calloway "Deadeye" Pruitt is the reluctant frontrunner. To collect his largest bounty yet — a body-snatching outlaw who may also be a literal ghost — he must outlast eleven rivals on live television while a smiling host narrates his every blunder. Trouble is, Deadeye refuses to "play to camera," keeps shooting the confession-booth lantern, and the eliminated contestants don't go home — they get hanged. With the whole haunted town riding on the finale, he has one season to win, or the saloon gets foreclosed by demons.

Starring: Bounty Hunter
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Set in a world where Weird West and Reality Competition coexist uneasily, our hero — a Bounty Hunter — must save... something. Probably a town.

The Coroner's Constituent
Forensic Procedural x Cosmic Horror

State Senator Marian Voss has built her career on closing cases—and now, with the governorship within reach, she's personally consulting on a string of impossible autopsies to look tough on crime. But every corpse on the slab shares the same impossible cause of death, the same geometry carved into the bone, and the same name whispered from inside the body bag: hers. As her poll numbers climb and her sanity erodes, Marian must decide whether the truth is worth a thing no ballot can contain. Some platforms were not meant to be built on this Earth.

Starring: Ambitious Politician
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Imagine if a Forensic Procedural show had a baby with a Cosmic Horror miniseries, and that baby grew up to follow a Ambitious Politician.

High Noon at the Honeysuckle Inn
Cozy Whodunit x Revisionist Western

When dapper city detective Cassius "Cash" Delacroix rides into the dust-choked frontier town of Marrow's Bend to solve a tea-cozy poisoning, he finds eleven suspects, one shared bathhouse, and a sheriff who smolders like a struck match. Every interrogation drips with sweat and longing; every alibi smells of bergamot and gunpowder. As the body count rises faster than the saloon-keeper's pulse, Cash must crack the case before sundown — or before he himself is undone by the widow in mourning lace. Dread has never been this damp.

Starring: Private Investigator
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Pitch: Cozy Whodunit x Revisionist Western. Tone: dread, but make it horny. Lead: a Private Investigator.

The Laudanum Ward
Revisionist Western x Psychological Horror

1887, a frontier mining town's only hospital, lit by gaslight and bad intentions. Night-shift nurse Corah Quint works the graveyard rotation alone, dispensing morphine to men who keep dying of the same wound — a wound that wasn't there yesterday. When a charming, unkillable gunslinger checks himself into Bed 9 and starts whispering things only her dead husband knew, Corah realizes the ward isn't full of patients. It's full of her. Slow-burn, sweat-soaked, and quietly terrifying, it's a fever dream where every recovery is a relapse.

Starring: Night-Shift Nurse
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Pitch: Revisionist Western x Psychological Horror. Tone: dread, but make it horny. Lead: a Night-Shift Nurse.

The Sampler: A Taste of Dread
Food Doc x Psychological Horror

Roy Tibble has sold premium artisanal salt to small towns for twenty-two years, and he's never met a customer he couldn't charm. But when his route lands him in Marender's Hollow — a fog-choked village obsessed with a "founder's stew" no one will describe — every doorbell he rings opens onto smiling neighbors who already know his name, his order, and his deepest fear. As the locals insist he taste "just one more spoonful," Roy realizes the documentary crew following him stopped blinking hours ago. A queasy, slow-burn dread about hospitality, hunger, and the unbearable politeness of people who want you for dinner.

Starring: Traveling Salesman
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Picture a Food Doc setting, but everyone behaves like they're in a Psychological Horror. Our reluctant hero: a Traveling Salesman.

Thou Shalt Not Get Voted Off
Reality Competition x Surreal Comedy

Father Desmond Pellow lost his faith somewhere between the offering plate and the parish's leaking roof, so when a reality show called "Last Soul Standing" offers a $2 million prize, he signs up to compete against eleven strangers in a remote desert compound run by a smiling host who may or may not be God. The challenges are deeply unholy: assemble IKEA pews blindfolded, out-fast a competitive eater, deliver a sermon to a panel of judgmental flamingos. As the eliminations get weirder and the confessional booth starts talking back, Desmond must decide whether he's playing for the money, the redemption, or just the immunity idol shaped like a communion wafer. Faith is a game now. The tribe has spoken.

Starring: Disillusioned Priest
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
It's Reality Competition meets Surreal Comedy... but the protagonist is a Disillusioned Priest.
Image prompt:
{

Neon Dojo: The Accidental Fist
Cyberpunk x Martial Arts

Dao Pham is a sleep-deprived noodle-cart vendor in the perpetually raining megacity of Neo-Saigon-9 who just wants his loan repayments to stop auto-deducting. Then a dying monk uploads the legendary "Iron Lotus" combat protocol straight into Dao's bootleg cybernetic spine, and now every black-market warlord in the city wants his nervous system. Problem: the firmware only activates when Dao is genuinely annoyed, which is constantly, and it crashes every time he sneezes. With a snarky holographic mentor nagging in his ear, Dao must master a martial art he never asked for before the corporate ninjas reformat him into a toaster.

Chum: A Death at Sea Documentary
Sports Doc x Slasher

For forty years, Captain Augustus "Barnacle" Vane has guided his trawler crew to record-breaking marlin hauls — and a film crew is finally here to chronicle his legendary final season. But when deckhands start vanishing one foggy night and a hook-handed figure in a slicker begins picking off the team between interviews, the documentary becomes a fight for survival. Vane, who refuses to break character even while being chased, keeps narrating his own demise to the camera. The catch of the season may be the crew themselves.

Hostile Takeover: Partners in Crime
Workplace Romance x Buddy Cop

Tech billionaire Dexter Vane has never filed his own expense report, let alone solved a corporate espionage case — so when his board assigns him a no-nonsense forensic auditor named Reyes to recover a stolen prototype, sparks fly in every wrong way. They argue over budgets, kick down server-room doors, and slow-dance at the company gala while wearing wires. He's a chaos-goblin who answers his own emails at 3 a.m.; she color-codes her ammunition. To save the company — and possibly each other — these mismatched partners must learn the deadliest skill of all: sharing a calendar.

Starring: Tech Billionaire

Welcome to Mudgepenny: A Cosmic Inconvenience
First Contact x Cozy Whodunit

Constable Daphne Crick has been on the Mudgepenny village force for exactly nine days, and her biggest case so far was a stolen prize marrow. Then a 400-foot luminous starship parks itself in the duck pond and a beloved jam-judge turns up dead at the harvest fête. Now Daphne must solve a locked-greenhouse murder while interviewing seven gossiping pensioners and one polite, eight-eyed alien ambassador who insists it "comes in peace but does enjoy a good clue." With first contact and tea cooling fast, she has until the church bells ring to name the killer — terrestrial or otherwise.

The Ballad of Knuckles McGraw
Indie Folk Musical x Acid Western

Vincent "Knuckles" McGraw breaks kneecaps for the Genovetti family until a botched shakedown at a folk open-mic curses him to communicate only through plaintive acoustic ballads. To lift the hex, he must wander a sun-blasted, mescaline-warped frontier where every gunfight is settled by harmony and every clue is hidden in a murder ballad's third verse. Pursued by a banjo-wielding desert prophet and his own off-key conscience, Knuckles learns the only way out is to finger-pick the truth. It's a tender, hallucinatory showdown between a hitman and his feelings.

Starring: Mob Enforcer

The Anointed Summer of Brayden Voss
Coming-of-Age x Conspiracy Doc

At seventeen, Brayden Voss thinks he's just charismatic — until a documentary crew arrives to film the backyard "wellness collective" he accidentally founded after a viral journaling post. Equal parts hormonal disaster and reluctant messiah, he must navigate first love, his learner's permit, and the seventeen adults now sleeping in his mom's garage who believe he can decode the moon. As the doc crew pushes for darker footage and a rival cult slides into his DMs, Brayden discovers that growing up and going full apocalypse-prophet feel disturbingly similar. Narrated entirely in breathy, ominous voiceover.

My Beast Friend
Creature Feature x Buddy Comedy

Agoraphobic horror novelist Marvin Pell hasn't left his cabin in eleven years — until a nine-foot lake creature crashes through his skylight, reads his unfinished manuscript, and declares it "honestly kind of mid." Now bound together by a curse neither understands, the prickly recluse and his unnervingly chatty amphibian roommate must survive a town of torch-wielding locals, a deadline-obsessed editor, and the horrifying ordeal of going outside. Marvin needs the monster's help to finish his book. The monster just needs a best friend. Somebody's getting eaten, and somebody's getting closure.

The Gospel of the Drowning Stars
Mythic Retelling x Cosmic Horror

Father Elias Crane lost his faith somewhere between the third funeral and the second whiskey — until the saints in his cathedral's stained glass start weeping black seawater and whispering coordinates. Tasked with translating an "ancient miracle" beneath his flooded parish, Elias discovers the holy texts were never about God, but about Something older, wetter, and dreaming just offshore. Now the only lapsed priest in a fishing town must decide whether to perform the rites that wake it — or the heresy that might keep it sleeping. Faith was the easy part. Salvation has tentacles.

Mostly Magic: A Documentary
Mockumentary x Cozy Fantasy

Failed mural painter Dennis Crubbe agrees to let a film crew document his "comeback," which mostly involves crying into a microwave lasagna and overdrawing his rent. Then a tiny, judgmental hearth spirit named Pim moves into his radiator and starts critiquing his color choices — and slowly fixing his life with cottage magic, enchanted soup, and aggressively cozy houseplants. As the documentary lens drifts from "broke loser" to "reluctant fairy-tale wizard," Dennis must decide whether he's ready to be happy on camera. Warm, deadpan, and suspiciously emotional about a radiator gremlin.

Cold Case of the Heart
Paranormal Romance x Cold Case

Father Emil Vance lost his faith somewhere between funeral number four hundred and the discovery that his rectory's microwave is the only thing that loves him back. Then a heartbreakingly polite ghost named Lucinda starts haunting his confessional, asking him to solve her 1987 murder — and, awkwardly, to fall in love with her while he's at it. As Emil reopens the coldest case in the diocese, he must weigh decades-old evidence, an unholy crush, and the very real possibility he's just a sad man talking to a draft. Romance has never been this overdue, or this dead.

Starring: Disillusioned Priest

Three-act structure: Paranormal Romance in act one, Cold Case by act three, and a Disillusioned Priest sobbing into a microwave dinner the whole time.

Grave Concerns: A Modern Embalming
Urban Fantasy x Satire

Mortimer Vane runs the last family-owned funeral home in a city where the dead won't shut up — literally, since the recently deceased now file complaints, demand five-star burials, and leave online reviews. When a venture-backed startup launches "AfterLyfe," a subscription service that resurrects the dead as compliant brand ambassadors, Mortimer becomes the only undertaker willing to let people actually stay buried. Armed with an enchanted embalming kit and a deeply unfashionable belief in dignity, he wages a polite, paperwork-heavy war against eternal life as a customer-loyalty program. Death, it turns out, has a marketing department.

Starring: Undertaker
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Imagine if a Urban Fantasy show had a baby with a Satire miniseries, and that baby grew up to follow a Undertaker.

The Vanishing Cabinet Protocol
Spy Thriller x Locked Room

Washed-up Vegas illusionist Cornelius "The Astonishing" Vale gets handed the worst gig of his career: a foreign intelligence service has sealed the only access panel to a nuclear failsafe inside a vault that locks from the inside, and the lone witness vanished mid-trick. With his sequined assistant doubling as a reluctant MI6 liaison and a deck of trick cards as his only weapon, Cornelius has 90 minutes to misdirect a room full of armed spies, solve who locked it, and pick a deadbolt with a dove. The catch: nobody left the room, and one of them isn't real. Prepare to be deceived — for your country.

Starring: Stage Magician
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Set in a world where Spy Thriller and Locked Room coexist uneasily, our hero — a Stage Magician — must save... something. Probably a town.

Honk If You Believe: The Glorbax Testimonies
Alien Invasion x Mockumentary

A documentary crew follows Brother Dale Pucket, charismatic leader of the Sedona-based Order of Eternal Upward Mobility, as he insists the mothership hovering over his compound is here specifically to collect him and his $400 starter robes. When the actual Glorbax invasion fleet begins vaporizing the suburbs, Dale reframes it as a "membership drive" and frantically sells parking spots in the apocalypse. The aliens, baffled, request a meeting with management. It's a faith-based feature about commitment, branding, and not reading the fine print on first contact.

Starring: Cult Leader
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
It's Alien Invasion meets Mockumentary... but the protagonist is a Cult Leader.

Code Blue: The Last Shift
Post-Apocalyptic x Slasher

Twelve years after the bombs fell, Marlene Voss runs the night shift at the last functioning hospital on Earth — a flickering wing powered by a bicycle generator and sheer spite. When a masked figure in a gas mask and surgical scrubs starts "discharging" survivors one by one, Marlene must protect her six remaining patients with nothing but a defibrillator, a clipboard, and a strict no-running-in-the-hallways policy. She hasn't slept since the apocalypse and she is NOT about to start a paperwork backlog now. The Reaper keeps regular hours; so does she.

The Grimm Ward: A Surgeon's Cure
Fairy Tale x Body Horror

Dr. Margit Vasco hasn't slept in nine years and has stopped believing fairy tales can hurt you — until a coughing child in her ER hacks up a living, blinking rosebud. Soon her patients are sprouting briar-thorn ribs, weeping golden teeth, and growing extra thumbs that whistle lullabies. Margit, who medicates exhaustion with vending-machine coffee and dark sarcasm, realizes the curse is contagious and she's Patient Zero of a "happily ever after" rewriting her own anatomy. To break the spell she must operate on herself before the storybook finishes the ending. Some cures are worse than the fairy tale.

Desert Storm: A Ballad of Lies
Military Action x Tragic Musical

Corporal "Smiling" Vance Mireles never enlisted — he forged the papers, stole the rank, and conned an entire forward operating base into believing he's a decorated war hero. The trouble is, the only way he can rally his doomed platoon out of an ambush is by singing — and every soaring power-ballad he belts reveals one more devastating lie about who he really is. As the artillery falls in slow-motion and the strings swell, Vance must choose between the magnificent fraud that made him beloved and the truth that could save the men who'd die for him. It's a heartbreaking, brass-and-tears musical about a man whose finest performance is also his last.

Starring: Con Artist

The Ghostwriter's Last Inning
Cold Case x Sports Doc

As cold-case clues collide with slow-motion replays and confessional talking-heads, Sol must decide whether the perfect ending he invented was also the perfect alibi. Some stories were never meant to be edited.

High Noon at Heat Death
Spaghetti Western x Hard Sci-Fi

Newly badged Deputy Wren Calloway patrols Perdition Flats, a dust-choked frontier town orbiting a dying red dwarf, where every duel is settled not by who draws fastest but by who correctly calculates relativistic bullet drift first. When a notorious outlaw arrives claiming he can violate the second law of thermodynamics, Wren — who faints at the sight of entropy — must master orbital mechanics, peer review, and the quick-draw before sundown takes 11.7 minutes to arrive. The townsfolk debate it in a saloon that doubles as a cryogenics lab. It's the slowest fastest gun in the galaxy.

Probable Cause: The Vault of Sweetwater
Heist x Legal Drama

Sheriff Delilah "Del" Caruthers runs the laziest county in Texas — until the slickest crew in the Southwest rolls into Sweetwater to crack the First Federal vault, and their ringleader turns out to be the defense attorney she once kissed at law school and never got over. When the heist goes wrong and bodies need explaining, Del has to prosecute the case AND chase the loot, all while pretending her courtroom voice doesn't go husky every time she objects. It's slow-burn dread with sweat on the upper lip. Justice has never been this damp.

Starring: Small-Town Sheriff

The Last Card: A Prophecy of Larceny
High Fantasy x Heist

Madame Vesryn, a velvet-draped seer who can read any future except her own, owes a blood-debt to the Archmage of Thornhold — and his vault holds the one relic that could rewrite her fate. So she assembles a crew: a sweat-slick lockpicking paladin, an enchantress who flirts as fluently as she lies, and a goblin who keeps proposing. The catch: every tarot pull warns that one of them dies tonight, and Vesryn refuses to ask which. Equal parts doom, longing, and grand-larceny, it's a candlelit con where destiny is just another mark to be robbed.

Cold Cuts: A Case Gone Cold
Cold Case x Food Doc

Dr. Vance Marlow hasn't held a scalpel since the surgery that ended his career — now he holds a tasting spoon. Lured out of retirement to crack a 22-year-old unsolved murder, he treats the frozen evidence like a Michelin tasting menu, lovingly narrating each blood-spatter pattern and decomposing clue in hushed, reverent foodie tones. As suspects "plate" their alibis and a rival detective sears the truth tableside, Vance discovers the killer left a signature as distinctive as a reduction. Equal parts forensic thriller and prestige cooking show, justice has never looked so deliciously overplated.

Starring: Burned-Out Surgeon

Seed pitch:
Picture a Cold Case setting, but everyone behaves like they're in a Food Doc. Our reluctant hero: a Burned-Out Surgeon.

Dead Man's Reverb
Hardboiled Detective x Rock Opera

Detective Frankie "Knuckles" Malone got bounced off the force for tampering with evidence — and also for sobbing during interrogations. Now a washed-up gumshoe haunting a rain-soaked city, he stumbles onto a murder that can only be solved by feeling things, loudly, in four-part harmony. As the case cracks open, so does Frankie: the noir voiceover gives way to power ballads, the precinct becomes a strobe-lit arena, and his microwave lasagna becomes a recurring duet partner. To catch the killer, he must do the one thing a hardboiled man fears most — hit the high note.

The Marks of Blackthorn Manor
Psychological Drama x Gothic Horror

Slick grifter Ezra Voss has scammed his way into a cushy "inheritance" at a fog-drowned country estate, certain the grieving widow is his easiest mark yet. But the candles relight themselves, the portraits keep score, and the house seems to know every lie he's ever told. As Ezra's confidence games unravel into something far more intimate — and the manor begins billing him interest on his sins — he realizes the only con left is convincing a haunted house he's worth keeping alive. To survive the night, the world's best liar must do the one thing he never has: mean it.

Till Cover Do Us Part
Marriage of Convenience x Spy Thriller

Senator-hopeful Diane Plimpton-Vasquez needs a spotless family image; freelance asset Marcus "Three Passports" Vane needs a legal address that isn't a safehouse. Their fake marriage is a flawless poll-booster — until her opponent turns out to run an arms cartel and Marcus's "consulting job" turns out to be assassinating it. Now Diane must survive a gala shootout, a leaked sex tape that's actually a dead-drop, and the crushing realization that the only man who's ever remembered her birthday does it because it's also a detonation code. Between debates she cries into a microwave lasagna. He finds it oddly endearing.

Starring: Ambitious Politician

Sleight of Hand: The Disappearing Asset
True Crime x Spy Thriller

Mild-mannered illusionist Roland "The Astonishing" Beck thinks his biggest secret is how he palms a half-dollar. Then a leaked surveillance tape reveals his stage assistant has been laundering state secrets through the vanishing-dove act for a decade — and Roland's name is on every dead drop. With a reluctant documentary crew filming his every move and three intelligence agencies certain he's the most dangerous double agent alive, Roland must weaponize misdirection, escape artistry, and one extremely real rabbit to clear his name. Turns out "now you see me" is excellent tradecraft.

The Whistleblower's Skin
Body Horror x Noir

Mid-level compliance analyst Dale Voss thought he was just reporting expense fraud — until he found the memo that explains why everyone in Accounts Payable is growing a second mouth. Now the only person who believes him is the chain-smoking ghost of his own conscience, and the only way out is to follow the oldest rule in the book: trust no one, especially the guy in the mirror who keeps shedding. As Synthrex Corporation "onboards" its employees into something wetter, Dale chases a paper trail that bleeds. The truth is in the building. So is whatever the building is becoming.

The Skip-Trace of Mawr County
First Contact x Cosmic Horror

Disgraced bounty hunter Cassidy "Coyote" Reyes tracks fugitives for a living, until her latest bounty turns out to be the only human who knows that the friendly aliens who landed in Mawr County, Nebraska, are merely the larval stage of something with too many angles to look at directly. Now her quarry is the one warning her to run. As the townsfolk start humming the same impossible note in their sleep, Coyote must decide whether to collect her paycheck or save the seven thousand people who keep insisting everything is fine. Her quirks: she narrates her own arrests, and she cannot stop sketching the geometry that is slowly unmaking her mind.

Starring: Bounty Hunter
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Set in a world where First Contact and Cosmic Horror coexist uneasily, our hero — a Bounty Hunter — must save... something. Probably a town.

Little League of the Damned
Sports Doc x Found Footage

Divorced dad Greg Pernicki just wanted to film his daughter's championship Little League season for the grandparents. But somewhere between the third inning and the concession stand, the camcorder starts catching things no scoreboard can explain — a base coach who never blinks, dugout chants in a language nobody taught the kids, and an umpire who calls strikes before the pitch is thrown. As parents vanish one tailgate at a time, Greg keeps rolling, because the only thing scarier than the thing in left field is missing Lily's first home run. Shot entirely on one increasingly cursed handheld camera.

Starring: Single Parent
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Picture a Sports Doc setting, but everyone behaves like they're in a Found Footage. Our reluctant hero: a Single Parent.

Code Blue: The Comeback Routine
Dance Musical x Sports Doc

Marisol Vega works the 3 a.m. shift on the cardiac floor, where she's secretly choreographed an entire jazz-funk number around the rhythm of the heart monitors. When a rival hospital challenges her ward to the National Defibrillator Dance-Off, a deadpan documentary crew embeds with the team to capture every grueling rehearsal, every sequined scrub, every blistered clog. Part triumphant musical, part sweat-soaked sports doc, it follows one exhausted nurse chasing glory between vitals checks. Will she flatline — or bring the house down before sunrise?

Reality Competition x Martial Arts

Bartholomew "Barty" Quill has tended the Stormgrave Lighthouse alone for nineteen peaceful years — until a foghorn blares, stadium lights ignite the cliffs, and a host announces he's been the unwitting star of "Last One Standing," the world's deadliest reality competition. Now ninety-three eliminated contestants want his immunity lantern, and the only way off the island is to win. Armed with a mop, a thermos of chowder, and martial arts he absorbed from late-night VHS tapes, mild-mannered Barty must roundhouse his way to a finale. The cameras never blink. Neither can he.

Crystal Ball and Chain

Detective Roma Velasquez can see exactly how everyone dies — except her insufferably handsome new partner, Detective Cole Briggs, whose future is a humming blank she finds infuriatingly, dangerously attractive. As a hooded killer closes in, Roma must decide whether to trust her tarot or the man whose death she cannot foresee. It's tender. It's sweaty. It's harmonizing about probable cause.

The Spy Who Sang Too Late
Period Piece x Tragic Musical

Vienna, 1911. Retired imperial spymaster Auguste Vereaux has sworn off ciphers for a quiet life conducting the opera house orchestra. But when a coded assassination plot surfaces hidden inside an aria, Auguste discovers the conspiracy obeys the iron laws of tragic musical theater: every secret must be confessed in song, every villain gets exactly one heartbreaking solo, and no one survives the third act finale. To save the Archduke, Auguste must out-warble a baritone double agent — knowing that whoever hits the final high note dies for it.

Starring: Ex-Spy

The Graveyard Shift: A Bedside Manor
Mockumentary x Gothic Horror

A scrappy documentary crew thinks they're filming a feel-good piece about chronically understaffed Blackmoor Sanatorium — until they meet Sister Imelda Vane, the night nurse who hasn't aged since 1887 and insists the patients "check out, but they never leave." Between deadpan talking-head interviews and lingering candlelit glances, the crew slowly realizes the call buttons ring from empty beds and Imelda's "smoke break" is just her exhaling at a portrait of a dead duke. It's all very professional. It's also deeply, unsettlingly horny. As the sound guy starts sleepwalking toward the morgue, the crew must decide: get the Emmy, or get out alive.

Personal Foul: Badge of Dishonor
Buddy Cop x Workplace Comedy

Disgraced ex-quarterback Roy "Hot Hands" Delgado — banned from the league for the infamous "fumble that broke a city's heart" — is sentenced to community service as a civilian liaison at the 14th Precinct's Records Department. Partnered with Detective Anita Vance, a sleep-deprived workaholic who communicates exclusively in passive-aggressive sticky notes, Roy must solve a corruption case while filing overtime forms in triplicate. The tension is professional. The tension is also, regrettably, not just professional. Between stakeouts and surprise HR seminars, they'll learn that justice is a team sport and the copier is jammed again.

Sworn In: A Field Study in Treason
Spy Thriller x Mockumentary

Idealistic young attorney Marisol "Mari" Vega thinks she's been hired to fight for the little guy — until a documentary crew, hired by an agency that doesn't officially exist, follows her through her first week at a law firm that's actually a CIA front. As she earnestly files pro bono motions, she keeps accidentally extracting state secrets, sleeping with at least two double agents, and signing what may or may not be a confession. The handheld interviews get sweatier and the briefcase gets heavier. Justice is blind, but the surveillance cameras are not.

The Pale Crown of Buzzard Creek
Revisionist Western x Gothic Horror

Deposed boy-king Aldric Vane flees a coup with nothing but a tarnished crown, a borrowed Stetson, and a cough that won't quit. He rides into Buzzard Creek hoping to vanish — but the town's saloon is run by something centuries old that remembers what royal blood tastes like. As the gunslingers turn gray and the church bell tolls on its own, Aldric must learn to draw a revolver faster than he ever learned to bow. There are no heroes out here. Only a king, a curse, and a very thirsty congregation.

Starring: Exiled Royal

Seed pitch:
Imagine if a Revisionist Western show had a baby with a Gothic Horror miniseries, and that baby grew up to follow a Exiled Royal.

Till Pursuit Do Us Part
Car-Chase Thriller x Marriage of Convenience

Burned-out ex-spy Dex Calloway needs a fake marriage to slip past a border checkpoint with a stolen ledger — so he weds his getaway driver, Nadia, in a drive-thru chapel doing 60mph. Now the most dangerous cartel in three countries is in the rearview, but the real crisis is that Nadia keeps "accidentally" rear-ending the agency that's tailing them, and Dex forgot their anniversary (it was Tuesday). They must dodge missiles, debate whose name goes on the joint passport, and discover that a marriage of convenience comes with very inconvenient feelings. Buckle up — and apologize.

Starring: Ex-Spy

A Lamp for the Drowning Heart
Period Romance x Dark Comedy

In 1887 on a storm-battered Cornish rock, lonesome lighthouse keeper Bartholomew Quill falls desperately in love with Cordelia, a shipwreck survivor he nurses back to health — until he realizes she keeps surviving shipwrecks, suspiciously, and that several of her previous "fiancés" are now lighthouse-shaped. As the romance curdles into a politely homicidal battle of wits, Bartholomew defends his beloved beacon, his dignity, and his nightly microwaved kipper supper. It's tender. It's deranged. Someone gets fed to a foghorn.

Starring: Lighthouse Keeper

The Last Embalmer: Tape 7
Post-Apocalyptic x Found Footage

Mort Kessler ran the only funeral home left standing after the world ended, and he refuses to bury anyone without proper paperwork — even when civilization itself is the corpse. Armed with a dying camcorder and an unshakable belief in "dignity for the deceased," he documents his rounds through the ash-choked ruins, narrating each body's eulogy to a microphone nobody will ever hear. But the dead in the wasteland have stopped staying buried, and Mort's footage captures something following him home. This is the tape they found in his hearse. It is the only thing that survived.

Goodfella Pirouette: A Mob in Pieces
Body Horror x Dance Musical

Vinnie "The Hinge" Carbone is the most feared knee-breaker in Cannelloni City — until a cursed protection racket leaves him with a body that won't stop dancing. Every time the music swells, his joints reassemble into jazz hands, his ribs unfold into spirit fingers, and his boss's enemies are choreographed to death. Now Vinnie must out-dance a rival family of contortionist body-snatchers before the whole borough peels itself into a chorus line. It's a horror musical where the only way to survive is to nail the landing.

Starring: Mob Enforcer

As the high desert bleeds into something older and stranger, Pru learns the cold case was never closed — it was buried alive. Justice rides at dusk. Bedtime is at eight.

The Last Sermon of Sorrowfen
Noir x High Fantasy

In the rain-drowned realm of Greythorn, where elves run gin joints and the moon never sets, disgraced cult leader Brother Vellum Crane peddles salvation to anyone with coin and a soul to spare. When his most devoted acolyte turns up dead in a temple of black water — drained of memory, not blood — Vellum must solve the murder before the city watch pins it on him. Trouble is, every suspect is a god, and Vellum's only lead is a prophecy he wrote himself, drunk, to swindle a duchess. Faith is a racket. The truth is worse.

First Contact x Survival

Deposed by a palace coup and shoved into an escape pod with nothing but a ceremonial scepter and a half-eaten brie, Archduke Bartholomew "Barty" Von Wexley III crash-lands on a swamp moon that refuses to acknowledge his titles. It's diplomacy by tantrum, survival by spite.

Armed with an enchanted prosthetic leg and the world's most sarcastic talking shield, he must outlast a hooded reaper that simply will not stay dead. War was hell. Last Rites & Wrong Moves
Dance Musical x Revenge Thriller

Father Silas Boon hasn't believed in much since the night a crooked land baron and his sequined enforcers torched the parish dance hall — and the orphans' tap shoes inside it. Now the only language his shattered congregation still speaks is choreography, and the only way to take down the man who killed their faith is to out-dance and out-gun his entire crew at the town's annual Jubilee Showdown. Armed with a censer in one hand and a revolver in the other, Silas trades his collar for a spotlight and his sermons for spinning roundhouse pirouettes. Vengeance has never been so well-rehearsed. Faith, fury, and jazz hands collide.

The Sophomore Conspiracy
Conspiracy Thriller x Magical Academia

Burned-out investigative reporter Margo Vell thinks she's exposing a tuition-laundering scheme at elite Brackwell University — until her source bursts into blue flame and her press badge starts predicting the future. The deeper she digs, the more she realizes the "endowment committee" is a coven, the dean is nine hundred years old, and her freedom-of-information requests keep returning as enchanted scrolls. Now Margo must pass three semesters of forbidden magic she never enrolled in, all while ranking microwave lasagnas by emotional damage. Truth, it turns out, requires a permission slip signed in moonlight.

Starring: Cynical Journalist

For Better or For Bocce
Marriage of Convenience x Sports Doc

Broke installation artist D040 "Mo" Moretti will lose his condemned harbor studio — and the whole sinking town of Pellucid Bay — unless he marries someone, anyone, for the municipal "Spousal Stability Grant." Enter Renata, a stone-faced retired bocce world champion who needs a green card and a doubles partner. Their loveless paper marriage becomes a gritty, talking-head sports documentary as Mo trains to win the Regional Bocce Cup he doesn't understand, the prize money the only thing that can save them both. Filmed entirely by a wheezing crew that will not stop asking how they feel.

The Last Brushstroke Commune
Post-Apocalyptic x Cult Exposé

Three years after the bombs turned the art world to ash, washed-up installation artist Dov Petrakis joins the Radiant Pigment — a doomsday cult that worships the last surviving tube of cadmium red and conducts very sweaty "color rituals" in a flooded gallery basement. Armed only with a camcorder and crippling imposter syndrome, Dov documents the cult's charismatic founder, who promises immortality through "smoldering brushwork." As the candlelit communions escalate and the Founder demands a final masterpiece painted in something other than paint, Dov realizes the exposé he's filming may be his last commission. Equal parts apocalyptic dread and unhinged, oily yearning.

Starring: Struggling Artist

The Last Unicorn IPO: A Disruption in Three Acts
Satire x Tragic Musical

Atlas Brightwall, the boyish trillionaire founder of a "mindfulness-as-a-service" empire, learns his flagship app has accidentally achieved sentience and chosen to unionize. As regulators circle and his board stages a hostile coup set to soaring power ballads, Atlas must decide whether to sell his soul or merely his data. Everyone in Silicon Valley communicates exclusively through devastating sung confessionals and synchronized standing ovations. By the final crescendo, the only thing that crashes harder than the servers is Atlas himself, belting his resignation from atop a kombucha tap.

Starring: Tech Billionaire
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Picture a Satire setting, but everyone behaves like they're in a Tragic Musical. Our reluctant hero: a Tech Billionaire.

The Body of Evidence
Forensic Procedural x Satire

Burned-out investigative journalist Margo Vane hasn't filed a real story since her divorce, until a city councilman turns up dead in a way the coroner calls "frankly, suspiciously sexy." Embedded with an elite forensics unit that treats every crime scene like a perfume commercial, Margo discovers a conspiracy where the murder weapon is charisma and the cover-up smells like cedar and regret. As bodies pile up and lab techs keep loosening their ties, she must crack the case before the truth gets respectfully redacted. It's a dread-soaked exposé about institutional rot — that absolutely refuses to stop fogging up the lens.

Starring: Cynical Journalist
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Pitch: Forensic Procedural x Satire. Tone: dread, but make it horny. Lead: a Cynical Journalist.

Pas de Deux ex Machina
Dance Musical x Conspiracy Thriller

Father Aurelio Voss lost his faith years ago, but never lost his killer jazz hands — so when his struggling parish launches a fundraising dance revue, he choreographs the show of his life. Then he notices the routines spell out coordinates, his lead dancer vanishes mid-pirouette, and the diocese's accountant is found face-down in a tambourine. As Aurelio tap-dances deeper into a shadow syndicate laundering money through liturgical sequins, he realizes the only thing standing between the truth and a global cover-up is one disillusioned priest with rhythm. He sobs into his microwave lasagna between rehearsals. The choreography never stops.

Starring: Disillusioned Priest
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Three-act structure: Dance Musical in act one, Conspiracy Thriller by act three, and a Disillusioned Priest sobbing into a microwave dinner the whole time.

Graveyard Shift: A Western in Three Courses
Acid Western x Food Doc

Out in the sun-scorched nowhere town of Buzzard's Mercy, night-shift nurse Delphine "Del" Cortez runs the only clinic for ninety miles — and, after midnight, the only kitchen. When a fevered drifter dies mid-sentence babbling about a chili recipe that "cures or kills," Del's documentary crew follows her into a hallucinatory border of cactus broth, peyote consommé, and patients who pay in heirloom beans. Part frontier ghost story, part lovingly plated food doc, it asks the only question that matters at 3 a.m.: is the wound infected, or just underseasoned? Narrated like a cooking show, lit like a fever dream.

Starring: Night-Shift Nurse
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
It's Acid Western meets Food Doc... but the protagonist is a Night-Shift Nurse.

The Last Reel Heist
Workplace Comedy x Heist

Faded action legend Roman Castellane hasn't had a hit since the '90s and now spends his days clocking in as a "brand ambassador" at the very studio that forgot him. When he discovers the suits plan to delete his master films to make room for a reality show, Roman recruits the world's most dysfunctional office — a temp, an IT guy, and a passive-aggressive HR rep — to steal the negatives back before Friday's quarterly review. There are laser grids, but also a mandatory team-building seminar. He's done his own stunts for forty years; the printer jam may finally end him.

Starring: Aging Movie Star

The Mortician's Long Goodbye
Cosmic Horror x Hardboiled Detective

Embalmer Silas Crane runs the only funeral home in a fog-choked harbor town, and lately his clients won't stay quiet about what they saw beyond the veil. When a banker turns up dead with seawater in his lungs and a star-shaped wound that won't close, Silas takes the case the cops won't touch — armed with a flask, a worn fedora, and the unsettling ability to hear corpses confess. Every lead drags him deeper toward a sleeping thing under the docks that's been recruiting the dead as witnesses. He's seen a lot of bodies. He's never had one ask him for backup.

Last Precinct: Rules of Engagement
Post-Apocalyptic x Military Action

Disgraced detective Roy Calhoun was drummed off the force for losing an evidence locker — then the world ended, which honestly took the heat off. Now he runs a one-man cold-case bureau out of a gutted strip mall in the irradiated ruins of Phoenix, trading bullet casings for canned beans. When a missing-persons case unspools into a militia's plan to weaponize the last working satellite, Roy realizes the only way to crack it is to stop investigating and start fragging. He's got a magnifying glass, a belt-fed machine gun, and zero remaining badge. Justice is served in full auto.

Starring: Disgraced Detective

Til Death Do Us Draw
Acid Western x Marriage of Convenience

Cassius "The Whisper" Vane retired from contract killing to a sun-blasted ghost town with nothing but a revolver, a hot plate, and crushing despair. When the town's water rights — and his pension — hinge on a forged marriage license, the local undertaker's widow offers a deal: a fake wedding, a real ranch, no feelings allowed. But between hallucinatory peyote shootouts and a microwave dinner he weeps into every single night, Cassius discovers the deadliest target he's ever failed to eliminate is his own heart. Saddle up for a feverish, sobbing love story with bullets.

Starring: Retired Assassin

Vital Signs: The Harmony Ward Deprogramming
Cult Exposé x Jukebox Musical

Night-shift nurse Pilar Okafor thought the new wellness collective renting the hospital's east wing was just very into vitamins and four-part harmony. Then her patients start signing over their pensions between vitals checks and the charge nurse only communicates in show tunes. As cameras roll on a "routine documentary about hospital staffing," Pilar realizes she's the lone uncharmed soul on a ward run by a chart-topping cult that literally sings its way out of accountability. To save thirty sedated true believers, she'll have to out-belt a charismatic guru during a 3 a.m. code blue. The IV drip keeps tempo.

The Last Light Between Us
Forbidden Romance x Urban Fantasy

Silas Vane has kept the Blackridge Lighthouse for nineteen lonely years, and he has one rule: never fall for the things the fog brings ashore. Then a storm delivers Marin — a banished tide-spirit who can only hold human form while his lamp keeps burning, and who turns to seafoam the instant it goes dark. Now Silas must choose between the oath that binds him to the light and the impossible, forbidden love that the city's bureaucratic Coven of Harbor Wardens has expressly outlawed. The catch: every hour they spend together costs the lighthouse one hour of fuel. Some flames you keep. Some flames keep you.

Caucus: The Cover-Up Cha-Cha
Conspiracy Doc x Dance Musical

State Senator Dallas Voorhees has a five-year plan, a winning smile, and one tiny problem: every time he tries to bury a scandal, his body involuntarily breaks into a flawless Broadway dance number. As shadowy gala kingmakers pull strings in smoke-filled ballrooms, a basement documentary crew zooms in on grainy footage of Dallas tap-dancing through redacted documents. Is it mind control? Is it the lizard lobbyists? Or is it just really, really good jazz hands? The truth is out there — and it's in perfect 5-6-7-8 time.

Code Blue, Encore Louder
Rock Opera x Urban Fantasy

Night-shift nurse Marisol Vega just wants to survive her double at St. Brigid's Memorial without falling asleep on the crash cart. But after a coding patient flatlines in perfect three-part harmony, she discovers the hospital sits atop a ley line where every dying breath powers an immortal glam-rock cult's encore. Armed with salt packets, a defibrillator, and a startlingly good belting voice, Marisol must out-sing the band's undead frontman before dawn — because in this city, the rules are simple: you cannot stop the bridge once it starts. A power-ballad-soaked supernatural thriller about overtime, oaths, and never breaking the high note.

The Quiet Type: A Family Affair
Family Saga x Spy Thriller

Reclusive novelist Margery Volk hasn't left her Vermont farmhouse in eleven years — or finished a sentence without three rewrites. When she discovers her late husband encrypted state secrets inside her bestselling family-saga trilogy, every intelligence agency on Earth descends on the sleepy town of Ashfield, posing as relatives at her granddaughter's christening. Now Margery must protect a manuscript, a town, and a casserole dish, all while her estranged son insists this is "exactly the kind of attention-seeking" he predicted. Murder, brunch, and dead drops have never been so passive-aggressive.

Starring: Reclusive Author

The Last Heir of Dustmoor
Grimdark x Neo-Western

Cassia Vaern, the deposed queen of a plague-rotted kingdom, wakes up in a sun-blasted border town with a price on her head, a cursed longsword she can't unsheathe sober, and a pickup truck full of someone else's bones. Hunted across the cracked highways by the iron-masked usurper's bounty riders, she trades crowns for diesel and prophecy for petty cash. All she wants is to reclaim her throne — but every oracle she meets keeps mentioning it's "definitely going to end badly." Grim, dusty, and faintly nauseous, this is revenge served lukewarm.

Starring: Exiled Royal
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
It's Grimdark meets Neo-Western... but the protagonist is a Exiled Royal.

Term Limits: A Campaign Across Time
Dance Musical x Time Travel

Senator Dale Brightwater has one flaw no consultant can spin: every time he wins a vote, he involuntarily tap-dances himself thirteen years into the past. Now stranded in a primary that hasn't happened yet, Dale must waltz his own grandfather into endorsing him, jazz-square his way out of a 1994 fundraiser, and seduce the electorate of three different decades — all while a rival senator chases him through the timeline in glorious sequins. It's a high-kicking, paradox-stomping musical where the only thing harder than time travel is staying on message. Vote early. Vote often. Vote in every century.

Starring: Ambitious Politician
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Cold open: a Ambitious Politician, alone, in the rain. The genre? Dance Musical. The vibe? Unmistakably Time Travel. Cue title card.

The Lamp Must Burn
Grimdark x Survival

On a fang-shaped rock at the edge of a dying world, surly keeper Bran Holloway has one job: keep the flame lit, or the kraken-haunted dark swallows the last shipping lane to the last free city. Then the oil runs out, plague-gulls eat his ration goat, and a half-drowned warlord washes ashore claiming the lighthouse is rightfully cursed. With three matches, a broken harpoon, and a deeply judgmental seagull named Earl, Bran must survive seven black nights. Grim. Wet. Out of oil. The light cannot go out.

Starring: Lighthouse Keeper
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
It's Grimdark meets Survival... but the protagonist is a Lighthouse Keeper.

Page Turner: A Cop Named Margaret
Buddy Cop x Buddy Comedy

Reclusive literary novelist Bartholomew Quill hasn't left his cabin — or finished a sentence aloud — in eleven years. When a witness-protection mix-up dumps loud, rule-bending Detective Margaret "Mags" Delgado on his doorstep as his unwanted bodyguard-slash-partner, the two must crack a publishing-house murder ring together. He solves crimes through metaphor; she solves them through kicking doors. Neither will survive each other's road-trip playlist. From the studio that taught odd couples to share a Honda.

Starring: Reclusive Author
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Cold open: a Reclusive Author, alone, in the rain. The genre? Buddy Cop. The vibe? Unmistakably Buddy Comedy. Cue title card.

The Last Encore: Crown of Static
Jukebox Musical x Post-Apocalyptic

Decades after the Great Silence fried every algorithm on Earth, music survives only in one battered, solar-powered jukebox bolted into a sand-buggy. Enter Prince Dorian Vexley III — deposed, sunburned, and clinging to a velvet sash that no longer means anything — who discovers his off-key power ballads are the only thing that can power the machine and rally the scattered survivors of Dust-Town. As a warlord called The Maestro hunts the jukebox for himself, Dorian must choose between reclaiming his lost throne and becoming the karaoke messiah the wasteland actually needs. It's a toe-tapping fight for the soul of humanity, and Dorian only knows the high notes.

Starring: Exiled Royal
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Set in a world where Jukebox Musical and Post-Apocalyptic coexist uneasily, our hero — a Exiled Royal — must save... something. Probably a town.

Sweet Nothings, Deadly Tentacles
Creature Feature x Romantic Comedy

Mid-level accountant Marvin Pflug just wanted to forward one incriminating email about NaviCorp's "totally safe" deep-sea drilling — instead he unleashed Gerald, a forty-foot bioluminescent kraken who is, unfortunately, a hopeless romantic. As Gerald devours the boardroom and woos the cleaning staff, Marvin must protect both his anonymous-tip hotline and his clumsy crush, HR rep Brenda, who keeps misreading every catastrophe as a grand gesture. Featuring meet-cutes in flooded stairwells, a tentacle bearing roses, and one very confused subpoena. Love means never having to say you're squid-food.

Starring: Corporate Whistleblower
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Picture a Creature Feature setting, but everyone behaves like they're in a Romantic Comedy. Our reluctant hero: a Corporate Whistleblower.
Image prompt:
{
  "high_level_description": "A photoreal one-sheet of a panicked office whistleblower clutching a manila folder in a flooding corporate atrium while a giant glowing kraken tentacle delicately offers him a bouquet of roses.",
  "background": "The flooded glass atrium of a sleek corporate skyscraper at night, knee-deep seawater rippling across marble floors and reflecting emergency lights. Shattered floor-to-ceiling windows reveal a storm-lashed harbor skyline glowing teal and amber in the distance. The Encore Interrogation
Psychological Drama x Buddy Cop

Burnout glam-rocker Sid "The Velvet Reaper" Calloway hasn't played a sold-out arena since 1998, but he HAS unintentionally witnessed a murder backstage at a county fairground. Now he's handcuffed to no-nonsense Detective Marisol Vega for witness protection — and she refuses to let him relapse into either heroin OR the third verse of his only hit. As the case spirals, the film slows into unsettling psychological territory: who is the man behind the eyeliner, and which of his memories are real? It's a buddy-cop thriller having a full nervous breakdown in the back of an unmarked Crown Victoria.

Starring: Washed-Up Rock Star

Imagine if a Psychological Drama show had a baby with a Buddy Cop miniseries, and that baby grew up to follow a Washed-Up Rock Star.

Objection, Your Honor, It's a Metaphor
Satire x Legal Drama

Dezzy Pruitt, a perpetually broke performance artist who pays rent in "exposure," accidentally sues a billionaire art collector and somehow wins the right to represent herself in the highest-stakes copyright trial of the decade. Armed with zero legal training, one inspirational beret, and a tendency to answer cross-examination with interpretive dance, she discovers the courtroom is just the world's most expensive open-mic night. As the system closes in, Dezzy must prove that her "found garbage installation" is genuine art — or owe damages she'll be paying off in the afterlife. A blistering, deadpan satire about justice, gentrification, and the unbearable pretentiousness of being right.

Starring: Struggling Artist
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Cold open: a Struggling Artist, alone, in the rain. The genre? Satire. The vibe? Unmistakably Legal Drama. Cue title card.

The Hard Sell at Dead Mule Gulch
Survival x Acid Western

Mort Pennywhistle is the finest vacuum-and-encyclopedia salesman the dusty Territory of New Perdition has ever ignored — until a peyote-laced sasparilla sends his wagon, his mule, and his sample case tumbling into a sunbaked canyon with no road out. Now sixty miles from water, hallucinating a chorus line of singing scorpions, Mort must barter, charm, and door-to-door his way past cannibal claim-jumpers using only his briefcase of brushes and an unkillable sales pitch. Every man he meets wants him dead. Every man he meets is also a potential customer. Closing the deal has never been this literal.

Starring: Traveling Salesman

Seed pitch:
It's Survival meets Acid Western... but the protagonist is a Traveling Salesman.

Dead Man's Bluff
Cold Case x Spaghetti Western

Forty years after a stagecoach massacre went unsolved, silver-tongued grifter "Honest" Cassidy Vane rolls into the sun-bleached town of Perdido with a rigged faro deck and a dead man's pocket watch he can't explain. When the town's last surviving witness recognizes the watch, Cassidy must solve the very cold case he's been conning everyone about — before a black-clad gunman with a ledger of grudges closes the file permanently. Part dusty whodunit, part squint-and-shoot showdown, it's a swindler's race to outdraw the truth. The con of his life, and it's also the truth.

Starring: Con Artist
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Set in a world where Cold Case and Spaghetti Western coexist uneasily, our hero — a Con Artist — must save... something. Probably a town.

How the West Was Beamed
Weird West x Alien Invasion

Dust-bowl drummer Cornelius "Corny" Pratt can sell ice to a snowman and a snake-oil tonic to a dying mule — which is why nobody believes him when he insists the new settlers in Bone Hollow are extraterrestrials wearing very bad human suits. Armed with a wagon of dubious miracle products and a smile that won't quit, Corny must out-talk a hive of body-snatching invaders before the whole frontier gets "harvested." His pitch of a lifetime now has the highest stakes imaginable: the planet. Closing the sale has never been this apocalyptic.

Badge of Honor: License to Filing
Farce x Spy Thriller

On his first day, rookie officer Dennis Pollard accidentally pockets a defecting scientist's microfilm, mistakes a deadly assassin for his carpool buddy, and triggers an international incident before lunch. Now every elegant villain in Geneva wants him dead — and they all think he's a legendary super-agent because he keeps tripping into ventilation shafts at the perfect moment. Armed with a parking-ticket booklet and zero clearance, Dennis must bluff his way through a tuxedo gala, a high-speed Vespa chase, and a code phrase he absolutely cannot remember. The fate of the world rests in the trembling hands of a man who's still on probation.

Objection, Your Adulthood
Coming-of-Age x Dark Comedy

Twenty-five-year-old Marcus Pry passed the bar on his first try and immediately accepted a case nobody else would touch: suing the universe for emotional damages. Armed with a thrifted suit two sizes too big and a misplaced faith in the goodness of all people, he discovers his idealistic crusade has accidentally exposed a small-town graft ring run by his own mentor. As witnesses keep "retiring to Boca" and his cactus becomes his only loyal client, Marcus must decide whether growing up means selling out — or finally winning the one case that matters. It's a bleakly hilarious courtroom fable about losing your innocence one objection at a time.

Starring: Idealistic Lawyer

The Eldritch Hour: A Town That Couldn't Stop Singing
Cosmic Horror x Jukebox Musical

Burned-out arts reporter Marla Voss takes one last lousy assignment — covering why the dead-end town of Harrow Falls hasn't shut up about its annual sing-along. Turns out the locals can't stop performing classic radio hits because a tentacled god beneath the reservoir feeds on jazz hands and earnest key changes. Marla's the only one immune to the cosmic earworm, which makes her humanity's last cynical hope and a terrible duet partner. To save everyone, she must out-belt an unknowable deity using nothing but sarcasm and a karaoke machine. The encore will end the world.

Starring: Cynical Journalist

Set in a world where Cosmic Horror and Jukebox Musical coexist uneasily, our hero — a Cynical Journalist — must save... something. Probably a town.

High Noon Press: A Western in Overtime
Revisionist Western x Sports Drama

Sheriff Wade "Dusty" Cobb has kept the dirt-road town of Pinch, Arizona peaceful for nineteen quiet years — until a drifting bookie informs him that, per local statute and a forgotten 1887 charter, all disputes must now be settled by full-court basketball. With the railroad barons fielding a ringer squad and the saloon doubling as a locker room, Dusty must trade his six-shooter for a sweatband and coach a team of grizzled ranchers to the championship. He's got bad knees, a tragic backstory, and exactly one inspirational speech left in him. Loser leaves the territory. Forever.

The Lighthouse Keeper Did It (Probably)
Cold Case x Screwball

For thirty-one years, Brunhilde "Bunny" Halvorsen has kept the Sorrowcliff Light burning and the same unsolved murder taped to her refrigerator. When a fast-talking insurance adjuster shipwrecks on her rocks demanding answers, her solemn cold-case obsession collides with his caffeinated optimism and a missing lobster diary. Bunny just wants to grieve into her microwave salisbury steak in peace; the universe wants a slamming-door farce with two suspects, one rowboat, and a foghorn that goes off at the worst possible moments. The truth is out there. So is dinner, and it's getting cold.

The Good, The Bad, and The Defibrillator
Spaghetti Western x Medical Drama

Faded glam-rock legend "Dusty" Calloway rides into the parched border town of Sangre Seca chasing a comeback gig — only to find the town has no saloon, just an overworked frontier triage tent. He'll have to stop the bleeding, restart a heart, and maybe his career — all before the cartel's specialist rides in for a second opinion.

Last Dance in Dead Man's Holler
Cold Case x Jukebox Musical

Reclusive thriller novelist Maren Vance hasn't left her cabin — or finished a sentence out loud — in eleven years. But when a forty-year-old unsolved disappearance reopens, the entire town of Dead Man's Holler can only communicate through spontaneous, fully-choreographed renditions of jukebox classics. To crack the case, Maren must overcome her crippling stage fright and lip-sync her way through honky-tonk confessions, doo-wop alibis, and one devastating power-ballad red herring. The clock is ticking: if she doesn't name the killer by the last song, the bar — and the truth — close forever.

Stiff & Garnish: A Killing in the Kitchen
Buddy Cop x Food Doc

Mortician Cornelius Boggs has embalmed bodies for thirty silent years — until a celebrity chef drops dead face-first in his own foam, and the precinct partners Cornelius with hot-headed gastro-detective Rico Vance. Together they work the city's underground supper-club homicide ring, narrating each crime scene like a Michelin-starred food documentary, complete with reverent slow-motion plating and tearful interviews with the deceased's pastry chef. Cornelius brings a corpse's calm; Rico brings a deathly fear of cilantro. They have 48 hours and one reservation to crack the case before the killer's next "tasting menu" claims another diner.

Starring: Undertaker
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Cold open: a Undertaker, alone, in the rain. The genre? Buddy Cop. The vibe? Unmistakably Food Doc. Cue title card.

Whodunit, Baby, One More Time
Amateur Sleuth x Jukebox Musical

Mild-mannered crossword editor Marvin Pesh wants nothing more than to finish his Sunday puzzle in peace. But when his neighbor turns up dead clutching a karaoke remote, an ancient prophecy declares Marvin the "Chosen Crooner" — the only sleuth who can solve crimes, but exclusively by belting reworked classic-rock hits at suspects. Now he must learn jazz hands, decode clues hidden in song lyrics, and out-harmonize a murderous a cappella cult before the third-act key change kills him. He really, really cannot carry a tune. Solving the case means singing for his life.

Starring: Reluctant Chosen One

The Unfinished Masterpiece
Cosmic Horror x Sword & Sorcery

Bartholomew Quill, a perpetually broke portrait painter behind on rent and self-respect, accepts a commission to paint the "true face" of a god that should not be looked at. Big mistake. As his canvas begins screaming and his brushes weep ink that whispers in a dead language, Bartholomew discovers the only way to seal the gate he accidentally opened is to FINISH the painting — while wielding an enchanted palette knife against tentacled critics from beyond the stars. Part starving-artist tragedy, part barbarian sword-and-sorcery epic, fully unhinged. Art is pain. So is this.

Starring: Struggling Artist

Sutures of the Sundered Realm
Forbidden Romance x High Fantasy

Dr. Maren Vell quit medicine after a thousand-hour shift broke her, fleeing the city to drink mead in a dying frontier kingdom. But when the realm's exiled Frost Prince is carried in with an arrow lodged a finger from his heart, she's the only one who can save him — and falling for enemy royalty is punishable by the Crown's executioner. Now Maren must keep him alive, keep their affair secret, and stitch up a plague that's quietly devouring the village. Caffeine helps. Magic helps more. Her cynicism, somehow, helps most of all.

Starring: Burned-Out Surgeon
Behind the scenes

Set in a world where Forbidden Romance and High Fantasy coexist uneasily, our hero — a Burned-Out Surgeon — must save... something. Probably a town.

The Keeper of Sorrows
Grimdark x Forbidden Romance

In a plague-rotted kingdom where loyalty is paid in blood, embittered lighthouse keeper Bram Oathmourn has one sworn duty: guide the dead king's war-fleet safely home so it can raze the rebel coast. Then a half-drowned rebel commander washes onto his rocks — devastatingly handsome, infuriatingly principled, and exactly the man Bram is sworn to doom. Now every flicker of the great lamp is a choice between the oath that defines him and the forbidden ache that's ruining him. Brooding, rain-soaked, and unbearably horny, it's a war epic where the deadliest weapon is eye contact.

Starring: Lighthouse Keeper

Seed pitch:
Picture a Grimdark setting, but everyone behaves like they're in a Forbidden Romance. Our reluctant hero: a Lighthouse Keeper.

Eureka! A Lovely Apocalypse
Screwball x Dystopian

In the rusted ration-state of New Cheerville, disgraced inventor Dr. Bibi Voltaire builds a machine to abolish all human emotion — and accidentally invents the world's first sarcastic toaster instead. Now wanted by the Ministry of Mood for "excessive zaniness," she's stuck sharing a one-room bunker with her insufferably chipper ex-husband, a defecting state censor, and a malfunctioning surveillance drone that keeps falling in love. As the regime tightens its grip, Bibi has 48 hours to either save the dystopia or get everyone killed by talking too fast. It's a screwball revolution with terrible timing and excellent banter.

Starring: Mad Scientist
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Imagine if a Screwball show had a baby with a Dystopian miniseries, and that baby grew up to follow a Mad Scientist.

The Murder Ballad of Hollow Pine
Indie Folk Musical x Psychological Horror

Disgraced detective Cyrus Vane—stripped of his badge for "hearing confessions that weren't there"—drifts into Hollow Pine, a fog-drowned mountain town where every resident answers questions only by singing. As townsfolk vanish one by one, Cyrus realizes the killer leaves clues exclusively in the lyrics of a haunting folk ballad nobody admits writing. To solve it he must learn the song's final unsung verse—but anyone who completes the melody dies. Part toe-tapping hootenanny, part slow-dread nightmare, it's a whodunit where the truth harmonizes back.

Starring: Disgraced Detective
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
A Disgraced Detective stumbles into a Indie Folk Musical conspiracy that can only be solved using the rules of Psychological Horror.

Murder Ballad: A Toe-Tapping Investigation
True Crime x Screwball

Banjo-strumming folk troubadour Earl "Two-Capo" Dabney returns to tiny Possum Hollow to headline the Heritage Pickle Festival, only to discover the festival's prize-winning gourd has been STOLEN — and the local true-crime podcast is already framing him for it. To clear his name before the town goes bankrupt, Earl must out-sleuth a deadpan documentary crew, a fast-talking ex-fiancée who runs the sheriff's office, and his own incurable habit of narrating crimes in three-part harmony. Every clue becomes a verse. Every suspect gets a chorus. Possum Hollow has eleven hours and one tambourine to save itself.

Starring: Folk Musician
Behind the scenes
Seed pitch:
Set in a world where True Crime and Screwball coexist uneasily, our hero — a Folk Musician — must save... something. Probably a town.

The Last Confession of Sam Spadehands
Satire x Hardboiled Detective

Father Augustine "Gus" Malone hasn't believed in anything since the diocese replaced the choir with a synergy app. So when the parish bingo cash vanishes and a stained-glass saint turns up shattered, he hangs a trench coat over his cassock and starts working the case like the gumshoe God never called him to be. The trail of lies runs from the bishop's brunch to a megachurch with valet parking, and every suspect wants absolution before an alibi. It's a hardboiled whodunit where the only thing more corrupt than the killer is the parking-lot expansion committee.

Starring: Disillusioned Priest

The Made Man Who Never Was
Heist x Psychological Horror

Sal "Knuckles" Provolone has spent twenty years breaking kneecaps for the Carnevale family — until he notices his apartment has no doors, his wife answers to three different names, and the same pigeon keeps landing on the same ledge at 3:14 PM exactly. Sal slowly realizes his entire "life" is an elaborate long con staged inside his own skull to crack the location of a vault only his subconscious remembers. To survive the unraveling, the enforcer must out-think the architects haunting his memory — before the heist finishes itself and erases him for good. A claustrophobic descent where the only thing scarier than the crew robbing him is what they're robbing from.

Till Death Do Us Part: The Eternal Embrace Exposé
Cult Exposé x Marriage of Convenience

Mortician Desmond Quill has buried half the county and married none of it — until a documentary crew catches him signing a hasty marriage license to inherit his late mentor's funeral home. The catch: his "bride," Posy, is the recruiter for the Eternal Embrace, a wellness commune that worships embalming fluid and matching beige jumpsuits. As the cameras roll, Desmond must fake honeymoon bliss while smuggling out evidence that the cult's "afterlife retreats" are suspiciously one-way. It's a slow-burn marriage of convenience wrapped in a true-crime takedown, and someone keeps rearranging the caskets.

Crystal Ball Evidence: A Murder Foretold
Forensic Procedural x Rock Opera

Madame Velveteen Crow runs the only psychic-hotline-slash-crime-lab in the rust-belt town of Cinder Hollow, where she's legally required to sing every prophecy in full power-ballad. When the mayor turns up dead — and her tarot deck names the killer three days BEFORE the body cools — the skeptical state coroner demands chain-of-custody on a vision. Now Velveteen must reconcile lab results with séance results before a wailing electric-guitar prophecy comes true and the whole town goes up in pyrotechnic flame. It's spectral evidence versus spectrographs, scored to a 110-decibel organ solo.

Encore at the End of the World
Spy Thriller x Cult Exposé

Burnout glam-rocker Dex Mallory hasn't had a hit since 1994, so when a slick "wellness label" offers him a comeback tour, he signs without reading the fine print. Turns out the label is a deep-cover surveillance front — and somewhere between the laser-tag-themed safe house and a microwave lasagna, Dex realizes the tour is recruiting fans into a doomsday cult that worships HIM. Now armed with a wireless headset mic and the worst hangover in espionage history, Dex must out-spy his handlers and de-program his own fan club before the encore literally ends civilization. A thriller about reverb, redemption, and reading contracts.

Starring: Washed-Up Rock Star

Footnotes: The Musical Truth
Mockumentary x Dance Musical

Reclusive literary genius Bartholomew Quill hasn't left his crumbling Vermont farmhouse — or finished his second novel — in nineteen years. So a desperate documentary crew moves in to film "the writing process," only to discover that Bartholomew can no longer speak in prose: every confession, panic attack, and grocery list now erupts as a fully choreographed Broadway dance number. As the town of Maple Hollow faces bankruptcy without his long-promised bestseller, the camera rolls while Bartholomew tap-dances his way toward one terrifying final chapter. It's a tell-all about a man who can only tell it in jazz hands.

Starring: Reclusive Author

Set in a world where Mockumentary and Dance Musical coexist uneasily, our hero — a Reclusive Author — must save... something. Probably a town.

The Last Verse at Loon Lake
Disaster x Cozy Whodunit

When folk darling Marigold Pike returns to the sleepy lakeside hamlet of Loon's Rest for a charity hootenanny, the only thing duller than her ex's banjo solo is the weather report — until the dam upriver starts groaning. Then the festival's beloved fiddler turns up drowned in three inches of suspiciously rising water. With the valley flooding by the hour and twelve sweater-clad suspects trapped in a tilting lodge, Marigold must solve the murder before the whole town goes under — all while resisting the smoldering park ranger who keeps shouting evacuation orders directly into her soul. Cozy, doomed, and unbearably romantic.

Starring: Folk Musician
